<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 2pt; padding-left: 2pt; font-size: 12pt; text-align: justify; width: 100%"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 45.75pt; width: 76.5pt"></TD></TR>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Tencent Music Entertainment Group Announces
First Quarter 2026&nbsp;Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">SHENZHEN, China, May 12, 2026 /PRNewswire/ -- Tencent
Music Entertainment Group (&ldquo;TME,&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;) (NYSE: TME and HKEX: 1698), the leading online music and audio
entertainment platform in China, today announced its unaudited financial results for the first quarter ended&nbsp;March 31, 2026.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>First Quarter 2026 Financial Highlights</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><B>Total revenues </B>were RMB7.90 billion (US$1.15
billion), representing a 7.3% year-over-year increase, primarily due to strong growth in revenues from music related services<SUP>1</SUP>.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Revenues
                                            from music related services<SUP>1</SUP></B> were RMB6.51 billion (US$944 million), representing
                                            12.2% year-over-year growth. <B>Revenues from membership services<SUP>2</SUP></B></FONT>
                                            <FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt">were RMB4.57 billion
                                            (US$662 million), representing 6.6% year-over-year growth. <B>Revenues from music related
                                            services other than membership services</B> were RMB1.94 billion (US$282 million), representing
                                            28.0% year-over-year growth.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">On an IFRS basis:</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 36pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 21pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Wingdings">&Oslash;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Net profit attributable to
equity holders of the Company </B>was RMB2.09 billion (US$303 million), compared with RMB4.29 billion in the same period of 2025, as the
Company has recognized a gain of RMB2.37 billion on deemed disposal of an associate in the first quarter of 2025.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 36pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 21pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Wingdings">&Oslash;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per ADS</B>
was RMB1.34 (US$0.19), compared with RMB2.77 in the same period of 2025.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">On a non-IFRS basis:</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 36pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 21pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Wingdings">&Oslash;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Adjusted
                                            EBITDA<SUP>3</SUP></B></FONT> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt">was
                                            RMB2.83 billion (US$410 million), representing 10.5% year-over-year growth.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 36pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 21pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Wingdings">&Oslash;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Non-IFRS net profit attributable
to equity holders of the Company<SUP>3</SUP></B> was RMB2.27 billion (US$330 million), representing 7.0% year-over-year growth.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 36pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 21pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Wingdings">&Oslash;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><B>Non-IFRS diluted earnings per ADS</B> was RMB1.46
(US$0.21), up from RMB1.37 in the same period of 2025.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><B>Total cash, cash equivalents, term deposits
and short-term investments</B> as of March 31, 2026 were RMB41.00 billion (US$5.94 billion).</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Mr. Cussion Pang, Executive Chairman of TME, commented,
&ldquo;This quarter&rsquo;s steady results reflect the effectiveness of our holistic approach to the music ecosystem. By expanding how
we serve and engage our audience, we have built a more diversified and resilient model, supported by continued strong growth beyond membership
services in our music related business. While AI is broadening participation in content creation, it does not replace human creativity
and, in many ways, reinforces the scarcity and intrinsic value of premium IP&mdash;which remains central to deeper engagement and greater
wallet share. Rooted in strong copyright protection, we are committed to channeling this value to elevate the creative economy, unlock
new opportunities across the music industry, and drive enduring long-term value.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>


<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><DIV ALIGN="LEFT" STYLE="margin-top: 3pt; margin-bottom: 3pt"><DIV STYLE="font-size: 1pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; width: 15%">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->





<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><SUP>1</SUP> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt; background-color: white">Starting
from the first quarter of 2026, &ldquo;online music services&rdquo; has been renamed to &ldquo;music related services&rdquo; to better
reflect the nature of our businesses included in this business line. Such change does not affect the amounts of our historical revenue
or its accounting treatment.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><SUP>2</SUP> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt; background-color: white">As
part of music related services, membership services primarily consist of membership fees paid for membership benefits and privileges,
including access to music and audio content, and other benefits and privileges within music related services. Revenues from membership
services for each quarter of 2025 were RMB4,284 million, RMB4,434 million, RMB4,564 million and RMB4,625 million, respectively. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><SUP>3</SUP> <FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt; background-color: white">See
the sections entitled &ldquo;Non-IFRS Financial Measures&rdquo; and &ldquo;Unaudited Non-IFRS Financial Measures&rdquo; for more information
about the non-IFRS measures referred to within this announcement. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Mr. Ross Liang, CEO of TME, continued, &ldquo;As
we operate in an increasingly competitive landscape, we remain focused on strengthening the resilience of our platform. Anchored by our
content-and-platform dual engine, we continue to bolster differentiation, drive engagement, and expand user lifetime value. Leveraging
Tencent&rsquo;s ecosystem, we are broadening user reach and deepening penetration, while advancing a tiered subscription strategy to better
address diverse user needs. During the quarter, we delivered continued improvement in SVIP adoption and user engagement. Together, these
initiatives position us to compete effectively while driving scalable growth and durable monetization over time.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>First Quarter 2026 Operational Highlights </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>CONTENT &ndash; To unlock long-term value, we
continued to invest in premium IP to drive differentiation and engagement, while leveraging AI to enrich content creation and improve
efficiency. </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 22pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt">Strengthened
                                            our premium evergreen catalog by renewing key label partnerships, including JVR Music, Linfair
                                            Records, and MOK-A-BYE BABY MUSIC LTD., securing access to iconic artists such as Jay Chou,
                                            Karen Mok, Harlem Yu, and Angela Zhang<SUP>4</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt">.
                                            We also deepened our strategic partnership with TF Entertainment through 30-day early release
                                            windows and expanded physical collaboration, reinforcing our content leadership and competitive
                                            differentiation. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 22pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Captured more user mindshare with our proprietary

drove incremental streams across our self-produced catalog and further enhanced its visibility.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

a multi-pronged approach and advanced a multi-tiered monetization strategy, including new offerings to capture demand for super-premium
music experiences. </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>First Quarter 2026 Financial Review </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Total revenues </B>increased by RMB539 million,
or 7.3%, to RMB7.90 billion (US$1.15 billion) from RMB7.36 billion in the same period of 2025.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><B>Revenues from music related services</B> increased
by 12.2% to RMB6.51 billion (US$944 million), compared with RMB5.80 billion in the same period of 2025. The increase was driven by solid
growth in revenues from m<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">embership services and offline performances related services, supplemented
by growth in revenues from advertising services. Revenues from membership services were RMB4.57 billion (US$662 million), representing
6.6% year-over-year growth, compared with RMB4.28 billion in the same period of 2025. The growth was mainly driven by our continuous expansion
of SVIP membership privileges, such as early access to offline performances and artist-related merchandise, and the launch of other new
membership programs, such as bubble, WeverseDM, and fan-club membership. Revenues from offline performances related services achieved
robust year-over-year growth. We successfully staged several successful concerts for our strategically collaborated local and Korean artists
across domestic and overseas markets. The year-over-year increase in revenues from advertising services was primarily due to our more
diversified product portfolio and innovative ad formats, such as ad-supported mode.</FONT></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; background-color: white"><B>Revenues from social
entertainment services and others</B> decreased by 11.0% to RMB1.38 billion (US$200 million) from RMB1.55 billion in the same period of
2025. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white"><B>Cost of
revenues</B> increased by 5.7% year-over-year to RMB4.35 billion (US$630 million), mainly due to increased costs related to offline performances,
advertising services and other IP related services. Meanwhile, revenue sharing fees decreased, resulting from declines in both revenue
sharing ratio and revenues from social entertainment services.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Gross margin</B> increased to 44.9% from 44.1%
in the same period of 2025, primarily due to increase in revenues from membership services, along with decreased channel fee.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Total operating expenses </B>increased by 5.9%
year-over-year to RMB1.21 billion (US$176 million). Operating expenses as a percentage of total revenues decreased to 15.3% from 15.5%
in the same period of 2025.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->3<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 2pt; padding-left: 2pt; font-size: 12pt; text-align: justify; width: 100%"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 45.75pt; width: 76.5pt"></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Selling and marketing expenses were RMB271 million
(US$39 million), representing a 36.2% year-over-year increase. The increase was primarily due to higher channel spending and content promotion
expenses.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">General and administrative expenses were RMB940
million (US$136 million), and remained relatively stable compared with the same period of 2025.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On an IFRS basis, <B>net profit </B>and <B>net
profit attributable to equity holders of the Company</B> for the first quarter of 2026 were RMB2.14 billion (US$310 million) and RMB2.09
billion (US$303 million), respectively. <B>Basic and diluted earnings per American Depositary Shares (&ldquo;ADS&rdquo;) </B>for the first
quarter of 2026 were RMB1.36 (US$0.20) and RMB1.34 (US$0.19), respectively. The Company had weighted averages of 1.54 billion basic and
1.56 billion diluted ADSs outstanding, respectively. Each ADS represents two of the Company&rsquo;s Class A ordinary shares.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On a non-IFRS basis, <B>adjusted EBITDA</B> for
the first quarter of 2026 were RMB2.83 billion (US$410 million). <B>Non-IFRS net profit </B>was RMB2.33 billion (US$338 million) and <B>non-IFRS
net profit attributable to equity holders of the Company</B> was RMB2.27 billion (US$330 million). <B>Non-IFRS basic and diluted earnings
per ADS</B> were RMB1.48 (US$0.21) and RMB1.46 (US$0.21), respectively. Please refer to the section in this press release titled &ldquo;Non-IFRS
Financial Measures&rdquo; for details.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">As of March 31, 2026, the combined balance of the
Company&rsquo;s <B>cash, cash equivalents, term deposits and short-term investments </B>amounted to RMB41.00 billion (US$5.94 billion),
compared with RMB38.04 billion as of December 31, 2025.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Declaration and Payment of 2025 Dividend</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On March 17, 2026, the Company&rsquo;s board of
directors declared a cash dividend of US$0.12 per ordinary share, or US$0.24 per ADS, for the year ended December 31, 2025, to holders
of record of ordinary shares and ADSs as of the close of business on April 2, 2026. The payment for the cash dividend of US$370 million
was made in April 2026.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Environmental, Social, and Governance (&ldquo;ESG&rdquo;) </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On April 20, 2026, we released our 2025 ESG Report,
detailing our progress in empowering creators, promoting digital inclusion, and driving sustainability across our value chain. These initiatives
have strengthened our ecosystem&rsquo;s resilience, leading to improved ESG ratings and broader recognition from our stakeholders.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Exchange Rate </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">This announcement contains translations of certain
RMB amounts into U.S. dollars (&ldquo;USD&rdquo;) at specified rates solely for the convenience of the reader. Unless otherwise stated,
all translations from RMB to USD were made at the rate of RMB6.8980 to US$1.00, the noon buying rate in effect on March 31, 2026, in the
H.10 statistical release of the Federal Reserve Board. The Company makes no representation that the RMB or USD amounts referred could
be converted into USD or RMB, as the case may be, at any particular rate or at all. For analytical presentation, all percentages are calculated
using the numbers presented in the financial statements contained in this earnings release.</P>

    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-bottom: 2pt; padding-left: 2pt; font-size: 12pt; text-align: justify; width: 100%"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 45.75pt; width: 76.5pt"></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Non-IFRS Financial Measures</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The Company uses non-IFRS financial measures for
the period, including non-IFRS net profit, adjusted EBITDA(inc.SBC) and adjusted EBITDA, in evaluating its operating results and for financial
and operational decision-making purposes. TME believes that non-IFRS financial measures help identify underlying trends in the Company&rsquo;s
business that could otherwise be distorted by the effect of certain expenses that the Company includes in its profit for the period. TME
believes that non-IFRS financial measures for the period provide useful information about its results of operations, enhances the overall
understanding of its past performance and future prospects and allows for greater visibility with respect to key metrics used by its management
in its financial and operational decision-making.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Non-IFRS financial measures for the period should
not be considered in isolation or construed as an alternative to operating profit, net profit for the period or any other measure of performance
or as an indicator of its operating performance. Investors are encouraged to review non-IFRS financial measures for the period and the
reconciliation to its most directly comparable IFRS measure. Non-IFRS financial measures for the period presented here may not be comparable
to similarly titled measures presented by other companies. Other companies may calculate similarly titled measures differently, limiting
their usefulness as comparative measures to the Company&rsquo;s data. TME encourages investors and others to review its financial information
in its entirety and not rely on a single financial measure.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Adjusted EBITDA(inc.SBC) for the period represents
net profit for the period excluding income tax expense, finance cost, share of profit/loss of associates and joint ventures, other gains/losses,
interest income, depreciation of property, plant and equipment and right-of-use assets, and amortization of intangible assets.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Adjusted EBITDA for the period represents net profit
for the period excluding income tax expense, finance cost, share of profit/loss of associates and joint ventures, other gains/losses,
interest income, depreciation of property, plant and equipment and right-of-use assets, amortization of intangible assets, and share-based
compensation expenses.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Non-IFRS net profit for the period represents profit
for the period excluding amortization of intangible and other assets arising from business acquisitions or combinations, share-based compensation
expenses, net losses/gains from investments and related income tax effects.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Please see the &ldquo;Unaudited Non-IFRS Financial
Measures&rdquo; included in this press release for a full reconciliation of adjusted EBITDA(inc.SBC), adjusted EBITDA and non-IFRS net
profit for the period to its net profit for the period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About Tencent Music Entertainment </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Tencent Music Entertainment Group (NYSE: TME and
HKEX: 1698) is the leading online music and audio entertainment platform in China, operating the country&rsquo;s highly popular and innovative
music apps: QQ Music, Kugou Music, Kuwo Music and WeSing. TME&rsquo;s mission is to create endless possibilities with music and technology.
TME&rsquo;s platform comprises online music, online audio, online karaoke, music-centric live streaming and online concert services, enabling
music fans to discover, listen, sing, watch, perform and socialize around music. For more information, please visit ir.tencentmusic.com.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>
